function lerJSON(raw) {
    var limpo = raw.replace(/```json|```/g, "").trim();
    try {
        return JSON.parse(limpo.slice(limpo.indexOf("{"), limpo.lastIndexOf("}") + 1));
    }
    catch (_) { }
    var posts = [];
    var a = limpo.indexOf("[");
    if (a !== -1) {
        var d = 0, s = -1;
        for (var i = a; i < limpo.length; i++) {
            var c = limpo[i];
            if (c === "{") {
                if (d === 0)
                    s = i;
                d++;
            }
            else if (c === "}") {
                d--;
                if (d === 0 && s !== -1) {
                    try {
                        posts.push(JSON.parse(limpo.slice(s, i + 1)));
                    }
                    catch (_) { }
                    s = -1;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    var foco = limpo.match(/"foco_do_dia"\s*:\s*"([^"]*)"/);
    return { foco_do_dia: foco ? foco[1] : "", posts: posts };
}
function chamarIA(_a) {

                        body: JSON.stringify({ model: "claude-haiku-4-5-20251001", max_tokens: maxTokens || 1000, system: system, messages: messages }),
                        signal: _ctrl ? _ctrl.signal : undefined,
                    }).then(function (r) { if (_to) clearTimeout(_to); return r; }).catch(function (err) {
                        if (_to) clearTimeout(_to);
                        if (err && err.name === "AbortError")
                            throw new Error("A IA demorou demais para responder (timeout). Verifique a chave da IA no Vercel.");
                        throw new Error("Nao foi possivel conectar na IA. Verifique a rota /api/claude e a chave no Vercel.");
                    })];
                case 1:
                    r = _e.sent();
                    return [4, r.json()];
                case 2:
                    j = _e.sent();
                    if (j.type === "error") {
                        tipo = ((_c = j.error) === null || _c === void 0 ? void 0 : _c.type) || "";
                        if (tipo === "rate_limit_error")
                            throw new Error("RATE_LIMIT");
                        if (tipo === "overloaded_error")
                            throw new Error("SOBRECARGA");
                        throw new Error("Erro da IA: " + (((_d = j.error) === null || _d === void 0 ? void 0 : _d.message) || tipo).slice(0, 120));
                    }
                    txt = (j.content || []).map(function (b) { return (b.type === "text" ? b.text : ""); }).join("\n");

}

                }
            }
            else if (event === "TOKEN_REFRESHED" && session) {
                setAuthed(true);
                setSbUid(session.user.id);
            }
            else if (event === "SIGNED_OUT") {
                jaCarregou = false;
                setAuthed(false);
                setSbUid(null);
                setPerfilLoad(false);
                setSbLoad(false);

    }

function MarcasScreen(_a) {

        var b = (profile.nicho || "").toLowerCase().trim();

    var combina = function (of) { return nichoMatch(of) && (!of.seguidoresMin || meus.seguidores >= of.seguidoresMin) && (!of.alcanceMin || meus.alcance >= of.alcanceMin); };

        React.createElement("p", { style: { fontSize: 11, color: C.mute, textAlign: "center", marginTop: 16, opacity: .7, lineHeight: 1.5 } }, "O pagamento da campanha fica retido com seguran\u00E7a at\u00E9 a entrega ser aprovada.")));

function DashboardMarca(_a) {
    var marcaProfile = _a.marcaProfile, ofertas = _a.ofertas, produtos = _a.produtos, vendas = _a.vendas, onIr = _a.onIr;
    var brl = function (n) { return Number(n || 0).toLocaleString("pt-BR", { style: "currency", currency: "BRL" }); };
    var mp = marcaProfile || {};
    var minhasCamp = (ofertas || []);
    var meusProd = (produtos || []).filter(function (p) { return p.dono === (mp.nome || "Marca"); });
    var vendasDeProd = function (pid) { return (vendas || []).filter(function (v) { return v.produtoId === pid; }).length; };
    var totalCamp = minhasCamp.length;
    var abertas = minhasCamp.filter(function (c) { return c.status !== "encerrada"; }).length;
    var allCands = minhasCamp.flatMap(function (of) { return (of.candidatos || []).map(function (c) { return (__assign(__assign({}, c), { campanha: of.titulo, valor: of.valor, bonus: of.bonus })); }); });
    var nCandidatos = allCands.length;
    var nAprovados = allCands.filter(function (c) { return c.status === "aprovado" || c.status === "entregue" || c.status === "concluido"; }).length;
    var nConcluidos = allCands.filter(function (c) { return c.status === "concluido"; }).length;
    var nDisputa = allCands.filter(function (c) { return c.status === "disputa"; }).length;
    var gastoTotal = allCands.filter(function (c) { return c.status === "concluido"; }).reduce(function (s, c) { return s + (c.valor || 0); }, 0);
    var comprometido = allCands.filter(function (c) { return ["aprovado", "entregue"].includes(c.status); }).reduce(function (s, c) { return s + (c.valor || 0); }, 0);
    var taxaPlatTotal = gastoTotal * 0.20;
    var vendasTotal = meusProd.reduce(function (s, p) { return s + vendasDeProd(p.id); }, 0);
    var receitaProd = meusProd.reduce(function (s, p) { return s + vendasDeProd(p.id) * p.preco * (1 - 0.05); }, 0);
    var barDataCamp = minhasCamp.slice(0, 6).map(function (c) { return ({
        label: c.titulo.length > 8 ? c.titulo.slice(0, 7) + "…" : c.titulo,
        value: (c.candidatos || []).filter(function (cd) { return cd.status === "concluido"; }).length,
    }); });
    var recente = __spreadArray(__spreadArray(__spreadArray([], __read(allCands.filter(function (c) { return c.status === "concluido"; }).slice(0, 3).map(function (c) { return ({ icon: "✅", texto: "Entrega aprovada: ".concat(c.nome, " em \"").concat(c.campanha, "\""), valor: c.valor }); })), false), __read(allCands.filter(function (c) { return c.status === "candidato"; }).slice(0, 2).map(function (c) { return ({ icon: "👤", texto: "Nova candidatura: ".concat(c.nome), valor: null }); })), false), __read(allCands.filter(function (c) { return c.status === "disputa"; }).slice(0, 2).map(function (c) { return ({ icon: "⚠️", texto: "Contesta\u00E7\u00E3o em an\u00E1lise: ".concat(c.nome), valor: null }); })), false).slice(0, 5);
    var dias7 = ["Dom", "Seg", "Ter", "Qua", "Qui", "Sex", "Sáb"];
    var hoje = new Date().getDay();
    var semana = __spreadArray([], __read(Array(7)), false).map(function (_, i) { return dias7[(hoje - 6 + i + 7) % 7]; });
    var tendencia = semana.map(function (lb, i) { return ({
        label: lb,
        value: parseFloat((gastoTotal * ((i + 1) / 7) * (0.7 + Math.sin(i * 0.8) * 0.15)).toFixed(2)),
    }); });
    if (gastoTotal > 0)
        tendencia[6].value = gastoTotal;
    return (React.createElement("div", { className: "rise", style: { paddingBottom: 24 } },
        React.createElement("h2", { className: "disp", style: { fontSize: 22, fontWeight: 800, margin: "16px 0 2px" } },
            "Ol\u00E1, ",
            mp.nome || "Marca",
            "! \uD83D\uDC4B"),
        React.createElement("p", { style: { fontSize: 13.5, color: C.mute, margin: "0 0 18px" } }, "Vis\u00E3o geral das suas campanhas e produtos."),
        React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "grid", gridTemplateColumns: "1fr 1fr", gap: 10, marginBottom: 16 } }, [
            { lb: "Investido", v: gastoTotal, cor: C.rose },
            { lb: "Comprometido", v: comprometido, cor: C.amber },
            { lb: "Taxa plataforma", v: taxaPlatTotal, cor: C.mute },
            { lb: "Receita produtos", v: receitaProd, cor: C.green },
        ].map(function (_a) {
            var lb = _a.lb, v = _a.v, cor = _a.cor;
            return (React.createElement("div", { key: lb, style: { borderRadius: 13, border: "1px solid ".concat(C.line), background: C.card, padding: "13px 14px" } },
                React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 11, color: C.mute, textTransform: "uppercase", letterSpacing: 1 } }, lb),
                React.createElement("div", { className: "disp", style: { fontSize: 20, fontWeight: 800, color: cor, marginTop: 4 } }, brl(v))));
        })),
        React.createElement("div", { style: { borderRadius: 14, border: "1px solid ".concat(C.line), background: C.card, padding: "14px 10px 6px", marginBottom: 14 } },
            React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", alignItems: "center", padding: "0 4px 8px" } },
                React.createElement("span", { className: "disp", style: { fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 700 } }, "\uD83D\uDCC8 Investimento na semana"),
                React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, color: C.rose } }, brl(gastoTotal))),
            gastoTotal > 0
                ? React.createElement(LineChart, { data: tendencia, cor: "var(--rose)" })
                : React.createElement("div", { style: { textAlign: "center", padding: "18px 0", color: C.mute, fontSize: 13 } }, "Nenhum investimento ainda. Crie sua primeira campanha! \uD83D\uDE80")),
        React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "grid", gridTemplateColumns: "1fr 1fr 1fr", gap: 8, marginBottom: 14 } }, [
            { lb: "Campanhas", v: totalCamp, icon: "📣", acao: function () { return onIr("campanhas"); } },
            { lb: "Abertas", v: abertas, icon: "🟢", acao: function () { return onIr("campanhas"); } },
            { lb: "Candidatos", v: nCandidatos, icon: "👥", acao: function () { return onIr("campanhas"); } },
            { lb: "Aprovados", v: nAprovados, icon: "✅", acao: null },
            { lb: "Concluídos", v: nConcluidos, icon: "🏆", acao: null },
            { lb: nDisputa > 0 ? "Em disputa ⚠️" : "Disputas", v: nDisputa, icon: "⚠️", acao: nDisputa > 0 ? function () { return onIr("campanhas"); } : null },
        ].map(function (_a) {
            var lb = _a.lb, v = _a.v, icon = _a.icon, acao = _a.acao;
            return (React.createElement("div", { key: lb, onClick: acao || undefined, style: { borderRadius: 12, border: "1px solid ".concat(lb.includes("disputa") && v > 0 ? C.rose : C.line), background: C.card, padding: "11px 8px", textAlign: "center", cursor: acao ? "pointer" : "default" } },
                React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 20 } }, icon),
                React.createElement("div", { className: "disp", style: { fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 800, color: lb.includes("disputa") && v > 0 ? C.rose : C.ink, marginTop: 2 } }, v),
                React.createElement("div", { style: { fontSize: 10.5, color: C.mute, marginTop: 2, lineHeight: 1.3 } }, lb)));
        })),
        barDataCamp.some(function (d) { return d.value > 0; }) && (React.createElement("div", { style: { borderRadius: 14, border: "1px solid ".concat(C.line), background: C.card, padding: "14px 10px 8px", marginBottom: 14 } },
            React.createElement("span", { className: "disp", style: { display: "block", fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 700, marginBottom: 10, padding: "0 4px" } }, "\uD83C\uDFC1 Entregas conclu\u00EDdas por campanha"),
            React.createElement(BarChart, { data: barDataCamp }))),
        meusProd.length > 0 && (React.createElement("div", { style: { borderRadius: 14, border: "1px solid ".concat(C.line), background: C.card, padding: "14px 10px 8px", marginBottom: 14 } },
            React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", alignItems: "center", padding: "0 4px 8px" } },
                React.createElement("span", { className: "disp", style: { fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 700 } }, "\uD83D\uDED2 Vendas dos seus produtos"),
                React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: 12, color: C.mute } },
                    vendasTotal,
                    " venda",
                    vendasTotal !== 1 ? "s" : "",
                    " \u00B7 ",
                    brl(receitaProd))),
            React.createElement(BarChart, { data: meusProd.map(function (p) { return ({ label: p.nome.length > 8 ? p.nome.slice(0, 7) + "…" : p.nome, value: vendasDeProd(p.id) }); }) }))),
        React.createElement("div", { style: { borderRadius: 14, border: "1px solid ".concat(C.line), background: C.card, padding: 14 } },
            React.createElement("span", { className: "disp", style: { display: "block", fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 700, marginBottom: 10 } }, "\uD83D\uDD50 Atividade recente"),
            recente.length === 0
                ? React.createElement("p", { style: { fontSize: 13, color: C.mute, margin: 0 } }, "Nenhuma atividade ainda. Crie uma campanha ou adicione produtos \u00E0 sua loja! \uD83D\uDE80")
                : recente.map(function (a, i) { return (React.createElement("div", { key: i, style: { display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", alignItems: "center", padding: "9px 0", borderBottom: i < recente.length - 1 ? "1px solid ".concat(C.line) : "none" } },

                        a.icon,
                        " ",
                        React.createElement("span", { style: { color: C.ink } }, a.texto)),
                    a.valor != null && React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, color: C.rose, flexShrink: 0, marginLeft: 8 } }, brl(a.valor)))); }))));

    var init = produto || { nome: "", foto: "", preco: "", comissao: "40", categoria: "", descricao: "", ativo: true, privado: false, temAfiliados: true, estoque: "" };
    var _b = __read(React.useState(init), 2), d = _b[0], setD = _b[1];
    var set = function (k, v) { return setD(function (o) {
        var _a;
        return (__assign(__assign({}, o), (_a = {}, _a[k] = v, _a)));
    }); };
    var ok = d.nome.trim() && d.preco;

                React.createElement("span", { className: "disp", style: { fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 800 } }, produto ? "Editar produto" : "Novo produto"),
                React.createElement("button", { onClick: onFechar, style: { background: "none", border: "none", color: "var(--mute)", fontSize: 26, cursor: "pointer", lineHeight: 1 } }, "\u00D7")),

"var(--accent)" : "var(--line)"), background: d.categoria === cat ? "rgba(168,85,247,.15)" : "transparent", color: d.categoria === cat ? "var(--accent)" : "var(--mute)" } }, cat)); })))),

    var _c = __read(React.useState(false), 2), loading = _c[0], setLoading = _c[1];

    var brl = function (n) { return Number(n || 0).toLocaleString("pt-BR", { style: "currency", currency: "BRL" }); };
    useEffect(function () {
        var sb = window._sb;
        if (!sb)
            return;
        setLoading(true);
        sb.from("profiles").select("id, nome, nicho, plataformas, publico, handles, foto_url, plano, aceita_convites").eq("papel", "criador").not("nome", "is", null)
            .then(function (_a) {
            var data = _a.data;
            if (data)
                setCriadores(data.map(function (c) { return ({
                    id: c.id, nome: c.nome, nicho: c.nicho || "",
                    seguidores: Number((c.handles || {}).seguidores_num) || 0,
                    alcance: Number((c.handles || {}).alcance_num) || 0,
                    eng: Number((c.handles || {}).eng_num) || 0,
                    publico: c.publico || "", plataformas: c.plataformas || [],
                    foto: c.foto_url || "", pro: c.plano === "Pro",
                    handles: c.handles || {},
                    aceitaConvites: c.aceita_convites === false ? false : true,
                }); }));

        });
    }, []);
    var _j = __read(React.useState(false), 2), criadoresFiltro = _j[0], setCriadoresFiltro = _j[1];
    var filtrados = criadores
        .filter(function (c) {
        if (busca) {
            var b = busca.toLowerCase().replace("@", "");
            var nome = (c.nome || "").toLowerCase();
            var nicho = (c.nicho || "").toLowerCase();
            var handlesStr = Object.keys(c.handles || {}).map(function (k) { return String((c.handles || {})[k] || "").toLowerCase(); }).join(" ");

        React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 10, marginTop: 14 } }, FERRAMENTAS.map(function (f) {

                React.createElement("span", { style: { marginLeft: "auto", color: C.mute, fontSize: 20, flexShrink: 0 } }, "›"));
        }))));

function BarChart(_a) {
    var data = _a.data;
    if (!data || !data.length)
        return null;
    var max = Math.max.apply(Math, __spreadArray([1], __read(data.map(function (d) { return d.value; })), false));
    var W = 300, H = 140, padX = 14, padB = 26, padT = 16;
    var bw = (W - padX * 2) / data.length;
    return (React.createElement("svg", { viewBox: "0 0 ".concat(W, " ").concat(H), width: "100%", style: { display: "block" } },
        React.createElement("defs", null,
            React.createElement("linearGradient", { id: "barGrad", x1: "0", y1: "0", x2: "0", y2: "1" },
                React.createElement("stop", { offset: "0", stopColor: "var(--accent)" }),
                React.createElement("stop", { offset: "1", stopColor: "var(--rose)" }))),
        React.createElement("line", { x1: padX, y1: H - padB, x2: W - padX, y2: H - padB, stroke: "var(--line)", strokeWidth: "1" }),
        data.map(function (d, i) {
            var h = (d.value / max) * (H - padB - padT);
            var w = Math.min(34, bw * 0.6);
            var x = padX + i * bw + (bw - w) / 2;
            var y = H - padB - h;
            return (React.createElement("g", { key: i },
                React.createElement("rect", { x: x, y: y, width: w, height: Math.max(h, 1), rx: "5", fill: "url(#barGrad)" }),
                React.createElement("text", { x: x + w / 2, y: y - 4, textAnchor: "middle", fontSize: "9.5", fontWeight: "700", fill: "var(--ink)" }, d.value),
                React.createElement("text", { x: x + w / 2, y: H - 9, textAnchor: "middle", fontSize: "8.5", fill: "var(--mute)" }, d.label)));
        })));
}

function LineChart(_a) {
    var data = _a.data, _b = _a.cor, cor = _b === void 0 ? "var(--accent)" : _b;
    if (!data || data.length < 2)
        return null;
    var W = 300, H = 100, padX = 10, padB = 20, padT = 12;
    var max = Math.max.apply(Math, __spreadArray([1], __read(data.map(function (d) { return d.value; })), false));
    var xs = data.map(function (_, i) { return padX + (i / (data.length - 1)) * (W - padX * 2); });
    var ys = data.map(function (d) { return H - padB - (d.value / max) * (H - padB - padT); });
    var path = xs.map(function (x, i) { return "".concat(i === 0 ? "M" : "L").concat(x.toFixed(1), ",").concat(ys[i].toFixed(1)); }).join(" ");
    var area = "".concat(path, " L").concat(xs[xs.length - 1].toFixed(1), ",").concat(H - padB, " L").concat(xs[0].toFixed(1), ",").concat(H - padB, " Z");
    return (React.createElement("svg", { viewBox: "0 0 ".concat(W, " ").concat(H), width: "100%", style: { display: "block" } },
        React.createElement("defs", null,
            React.createElement("linearGradient", { id: "areaGrad", x1: "0", y1: "0", x2: "0", y2: "1" },
                React.createElement("stop", { offset: "0", stopColor: cor, stopOpacity: "0.25" }),
                React.createElement("stop", { offset: "1", stopColor: cor, stopOpacity: "0" }))),
        React.createElement("path", { d: area, fill: "url(#areaGrad)" }),
        React.createElement("path", { d: path, fill: "none", stroke: cor, strokeWidth: "2.2", strokeLinejoin: "round", strokeLinecap: "round" }),
        data.map(function (d, i) { return (React.createElement("g", { key: i },
            React.createElement("circle", { cx: xs[i], cy: ys[i], r: "3.2", fill: cor }),
            React.createElement("text", { x: xs[i], y: H - 5, textAnchor: "middle", fontSize: "8", fill: "var(--mute)" }, d.label))); })));
}

function Input(_a) {

function FotoUpload(_a) {
    var value = _a.value, onChange = _a.onChange, _b = _a.size, size = _b === void 0 ? 76 : _b, redondo = _a.redondo, _c = _a.rotulo, rotulo = _c === void 0 ? "Adicionar foto" : _c;
    var _d = __read(React.useState(false), 2), enviando = _d[0], setEnviando = _d[1];
    var onFile = function (e) {
        var f = e.target.files && e.target.files[0];
        if (!f)
            return;
        var sb = window._sb;
        if (!sb || !sb.storage) {
            var r = new FileReader();
            r.onload = function () { return onChange(r.result); };
            r.readAsDataURL(f);
            return;
        }
        setEnviando(true);
        var ext = (f.name && f.name.indexOf(".") >= 0) ? f.name.split(".").pop() : "jpg";
        var caminho = "img_" + Date.now() + "_" + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8) + "." + ext;
        sb.storage.from("imagens").upload(caminho, f, { cacheControl: "3600", upsert: true }).then(function (res) {
            if (res.error) {
                setEnviando(false);
                try { window.alert("Erro ao enviar imagem: " + res.error.message); } catch (ee) { }
                return;
            }
            var pub = sb.storage.from("imagens").getPublicUrl(caminho);
            var url = pub && pub.data && pub.data.publicUrl;
            setEnviando(false);
            if (url)
                onChange(url);
        }).catch(function (err) {
            setEnviando(false);
            try { window.alert("Erro ao enviar imagem: " + (err && err.message ? err.message : err)); } catch (ee) { }
        });
    };
    return (React.createElement("label", { style: { display: "inline-flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 12, cursor: "pointer" } },
        React.createElement("span", { style: { width: size, height: size, borderRadius: redondo ? "50%" : 14, overflow: "hidden", border: "1px dashed ".concat(C.line), background: C.soft, display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", flexShrink: 0 } }, enviando ? React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: 11, color: C.amber } }, "...") : value ? React.createElement("img", { src: value, alt: "", style: { width: "100%", height: "100%", objectFit: "cover" } }) : React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: 22, color: C.mute } }, "\uFF0B")),
        React.createElement("span", { style: { fontSize: 13, color: C.amber, fontWeight: 600 } }, enviando ? "Enviando..." : value ? "Trocar foto" : rotulo),
        React.createElement("input", { type: "file", accept: "image/*", onChange: onFile, style: { display: "none" } })));
}

function Chips(_a) {
    var options = _a.options, value = _a.value, onChange = _a.onChange, multi = _a.multi;
    var toggle = function (o) {
        if (!multi)
            return onChange(o);
        onChange(value.includes(o) ? value.filter(function (x) { return x !== o; }) : __spreadArray(__spreadArray([], __read(value), false), [o], false));
    };
    return (React.createElement("div", { style: { display: "flex", flexWrap: "wrap", gap: 8 } }, options.map(function (o) {
        var on = multi ? value.includes(o) : value === o;
        return (React.createElement("button", { key: o, onClick: function () { return toggle(o); }, style: {
                padding: "9px 14px", borderRadius: 11, cursor: "pointer", fontSize: 13.5, fontWeight: 600, fontFamily: "'DM Sans', sans-serif", transition: "all .15s",
                border: "1px solid ".concat(on ? C.amber : C.line),
                background: on ? "linear-gradient(135deg, ".concat(C.amber, ", ").concat(C.amberDeep, ")") : "transparent",
                color: on ? "var(--onAccent)" : C.ink,
            } }, o));
    })));
}
function Botao(_a) {
    var children = _a.children, onClick = _a.onClick, disabled = _a.disabled, style = _a.style;
    return (React.createElement("button", { onClick: onClick, disabled: disabled, style: __assign({ width: "100%", padding: "14px 18px", borderRadius: 12, border: "none", cursor: disabled ? "default" : "pointer", fontFamily: "'DM Sans', sans-serif", fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 700, marginTop: 22, transition: "opacity .2s", background: disabled ? C.line : "linear-gradient(135deg, ".concat(C.amber, ", ").concat(C.amberDeep, ")"), color: disabled ? C.mute : "var(--onAccent)", opacity: disabled ? 0.7 : 1 }, style) }, children));
}
function Bloco(_a) {
